<gmapID>0x80c3686a005923d7:0x3078b59cd13c2beb< /gmapID>< Review>
The food is very good. The chef Freedom, has a love of food, and the soups made that day are awesome ( french onion, vegy beef, etc...). Fish and chips had a huge portion of fish moist and tender. The cook made the tarter for us and delivered it to the table as he says "with love". Great service and well lit unlike the othelr dingy sports bars in the area we have been to. We are here for 3 weeks from out of town, and have been looking for a place like this.  Many tv's to watch sporting events. Whatever the sporting event, you can watch it here.  Watch out for other reviews put out by other local bars trying to discourage you for coming here. Try it once and make a decsion for yourself.< /Review>

Love the pleasant, welcoming team and atmosphere here!  It's set up cozy and much more spacious than other businesses in this packing house complex.  The two young ladies were so sweet and helpful this morning after 9 am.

< Text>
I had potentially a very difficult day that was transformed into a most pleasant experience.

I was on a family road trip and my car engine started knocking in Buttonwillow, CA.  The closest civilization: Bakersfield.  I drove the vehicle as far as I could and had it towed the rest of the way to the only shop I could find with my crappy cell service that was open on a Saturday evening and within the stupid 7 mile limit of basic AAA (that will be another review).

We drop off the car I go in, and say, "Help."  And help they did!  Not the car, mind you.  It was beyond the pale.  I was told it was probably an internal engine problem that would require a rebuild and that they could not do it until after the weekend.  Frankly, it wasn't worth doing.

Ugly problem?  Got worse.  Since I was 800 miles from my destination I had to find a car to rent to get the six of us home or a hotel so I could find one tomorrow.  The search was becoming fruitless.  "We are all full."  "We can't accommodate that many."  "We have no rental cars of that size, maybe tomorrow?"  What was I do?

Well the staff did everything they could.  They called rental agencies, they looked up hotels for me, one extremely kind employee offered to clock out and take us to a rental car agency.

Short story (too late?).  I found a hotel, got a car the next day and headed home.  Abandoning my dead car in their parking lot, promising to get rid of it.  Only to find out none of the salvage yards I called wanted it, even for free!  Some even refused to call me back (more reviews).  I kept the folks here updated and eventually donated it to Habitat for Humanity.

So a review that has little to do with auto service?  Yes, indeed.   As someone from out of town who could offer them nothing but the cost of my diagnostic, they went far above and beyond.  You have every reason to expect kind and courteous service from these folks.  If you are tired of dishonest mechanics who seem to care only for how much they can get out of you, I recommend using this shop.  And if you are the boss reading this, give these guys a raise, or whatever it takes to hold on to them.  They are gold!< /Text>

< Review>
Our Experience with the Sawl Law Group was only positive.  My adult son was in serious trouble and refused to follow our extended family's advice on how to plea, so as to enable him to get the help we thought he needed.  Martin Taleisnik represented us and went above and beyond his call-to-duty in repeatedly meeting with our son and trying to talk sense into him.  Because of his familiarity with the D.A.'s and judges, he was able to counsel us as to what to expect and whom to avoid, if possible.

All we were concerned about was that my son would get a fair hearing and not be swept aside by the court process.  During one court appearance, Mr. Taleisnik was in the judge's chambers for over 20 minutes, presenting the mitigating factors in my son's case.  At the sentencing hearing, he gave an impassioned speech to the judge which persuaded the judge to give him probation.  During that speech, a female sitting behind us in court tapped us on the shoulder and told us that she was impressed by our attorney.

Regarding the fee.  We were quoted a reasonable global fee that would cover anything that would transpire, short of a trial.  My son's case was continued almost monthly for 6 months, due to his co-defendant and other court procedures.  Mr. Taleisnik was always there, on time, and would speak to us afterward in the hall, at length, about what the proceedings meant and what the next step was.

I highly recommend Martin Taleisnik to anyone needing legal representation and would seek him out again,  if needed.< /Review>

<Rate>1< /Rate><Review>My experience with Big Daddys Army Surplus store was terrible.   I looked at the reviews posted here and since my experience here I now believe that the reviews are made up.  They all hit on 2 or 3 things which like "the owner is great, you can find everything you need".  The reason I believe these are made up is because the same points that they say are exactly what the store is lacking.  The owner was rude, there are no prices on the majority of items, there is barely any room to walk around the store, the hours of operation were not followed (I had to call the store an hour after the store was supposed to be open" and the owner said he would be there in ten minutes.  I went to a few other nearby stores to wait and the stores all chuckled a bit and said he always opens late.  25 minutes later he opened up.  I had to ask for the price on every item because they were not posted which he very obviously tailors the price based on his belief of how much one could pay.

For example, I was wearing a tie and coat and when I asked him the price of a used Molle 2 assault pack he told me $160.  First of all you can buy a new one for less than that
Also, I have been shopping for those for a while and didn't need one but wanted to see how his prices match up with the rest of reputable businesses.  When he told me the price I said "are you serious?" Then he said "yes, why?".  I then told him that you can buy used molle 2 assault packs online for $32.  I know all because of my prior shopping.  These were from actual businesses not private people selling just one or two.  I asked him about other items and their prices and they were all extremely over priced.  I left and will never return.

If you still decide to shop there do so at your own risk.  If you do go I suggest bringing your smartphone and after asking for the price of an item look it up on Amazon or another online resource to compare prices.
